from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
import shutil
import subprocess
from typing import Any
from typing import Optional

from PIL import Image

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def ffmpeg_exists() -> bool:
    return shutil.which("ffmpeg") is not None


def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    try:
        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
        if completed.returncode == 0:
            return True, ""
        return False, completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"
    except Exception as exc:
        return False, str(exc)


def _render_title_overlay_image(output_path: str, width: int, height: int, lines: list[str]) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    # Deterministic PNG placeholder artifact for compatibility-only phase.
    try:
        _write_placeholder_png(Path(output_path), "cover_overlay", lines, width=width, height=height)
        return True, ""
    except Exception as exc:
        return False, str(exc)


def _write_placeholder_png(path: Path, label: str, lines: list[str], width: int = 1280, height: int = 720) -> None:
    seed = f"{label}|{'|'.join(lines)}".encode("utf-8")
    checksum = sum(seed) % 256
    color = ((checksum * 3) % 256, (checksum * 5) % 256, (checksum * 7) % 256)
    image = Image.new("RGB", (width, height), color=color)
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    image.save(path, format="PNG")


def run_stage8_cover(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage8 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    raw_cover_titles = info.get("cover_titles") if isinstance(info.get("cover_titles"), list) else []
    cover_titles: list[str] = []
    for item in raw_cover_titles:
        if isinstance(item, dict):
            text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
        else:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
        if text:
            cover_titles.append(text)
    if not cover_titles:
        for key in ("cover_title_up", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "cover_title_middle", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "cover_title_down", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?):
            text = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
            if text:
                cover_titles.append(text)

    title_txt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_title", ".txt")
    title_txt.write_text("\n".join(cover_titles) + ("\n" if cover_titles else ""), encoding="utf-8")
    output_video = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover", ".mp4")
    overlay_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_overlay", ".png")
    cover_image_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_image", ".png")
    cover_preview_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_preview", ".png")
    subtitle_preview_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_subtitle_preview", ".png")
    style_preview_sheet_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_style_preview_sheet", ".png")
    overlay_assets_manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_overlay_assets_manifest", ".json")
    subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_correct_subtitles", ".srt")
    if not subtitle_for_timing.exists():
        subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")

    method = "title_text_only"
    overlay_duration_seconds = 0.0
    fallback_used = False
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    overlay_rendered = False
    overlay_render_error = ""
    overlay_ok, overlay_err = _render_title_overlay_image(str(overlay_path), 1280, 720, cover_titles)
    if overlay_ok and overlay_path.exists():
        overlay_rendered = True
    elif overlay_err:
        overlay_render_error = str(overlay_err)

    if not overlay_path.exists():
        _write_placeholder_png(overlay_path, "cover_overlay_fallback", cover_titles)

    if overlay_path.exists():
        shutil.copyfile(overlay_path, cover_image_path)
    else:
        _write_placeholder_png(cover_image_path, "cover_image", cover_titles)
    _write_placeholder_png(cover_preview_path, "cover_preview", cover_titles)
    _write_placeholder_png(subtitle_preview_path, "subtitle_preview", cover_titles)
    _write_placeholder_png(style_preview_sheet_path, "style_preview_sheet", cover_titles)

    if ffmpeg_exists() and overlay_rendered:
        overlay_duration_seconds = 1.7 if subtitle_for_timing.exists() else 2.0
        filter_expr = f"[0:v][1:v]overlay=0:0:enable='between(t,0,{overlay_duration_seconds:.3f})'"
        ok, err = run_ffmpeg(
            ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-i", str(overlay_path), "-filter_complex", filter_expr, str(output_video)]
        )
        if ok and output_video.exists():
            method = "video_title_overlay"
        else:
            fallback_used = True
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)
    else:
        fallback_used = True
        if ffmpeg_exists() and not overlay_rendered:
            method = "overlay_render_failed"
        if strict:
            method = "strict_rejected"
        else:
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)

    strict_rejected = strict and fallback_used
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "cover_titles": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_lines": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_up": str(info.get("cover_title_up", "")),
        "cover_title_middle": str(info.get("cover_title_middle", "")),
        "cover_title_down": str(info.get("cover_title_down", "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "method": method,
        "fallback_used": fallback_used,
        "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
        "overlay_duration_seconds": overlay_duration_seconds,
        "overlay_rendered": overlay_rendered,
        "overlay_render_error": overlay_render_error,
        "overlay_path": str(overlay_path) if overlay_path.exists() else "",
        "cover_image_path": str(cover_image_path),
        "cover_preview_image_path": str(cover_preview_path),
        "subtitle_preview_image_path": str(subtitle_preview_path),
        "style_preview_sheet_path": str(style_preview_sheet_path),
        "overlay_assets_manifest_path": str(overlay_assets_manifest_path),
    }
    overlay_assets_payload = {
        "schema_version": "1.0",
        "task_id": task_id,
        "coordinate_space": "pixel_on_reference_canvas",
        "reference_video_role": "master_video",
        "canvas_width": 1280,
        "canvas_height": 720,
        "overlays": [
            {
                "kind": "cover_overlay",
                "asset_id": "cover_overlay",
                "source_artifact_id": "cover_overlay_image",
                "asset_download_url": None,
                "start": 0.0,
                "end": None,
                "x": 0,
                "y": 0,
                "width": 1280,
                "height": 720,
                "opacity": 1.0,
                "z_index": 10,
                "source": "generated",
            }
        ],
    }
    overlay_assets_manifest_path.write_text(
        json.dumps(overlay_assets_payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_manifest", ".json")
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(
        success=not strict_rejected,
        output_file=str(output_video if output_video.exists() else source),
        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage8 fallback" if strict_rejected else None,
        artifacts={
            "manifest_file": str(manifest_path),
            "overlay_assets_manifest": str(overlay_assets_manifest_path),
            "cover_overlay_image": str(overlay_path),
            "cover_image": str(cover_image_path),
            "cover_preview_image": str(cover_preview_path),
            "subtitle_preview_image": str(subtitle_preview_path),
            "style_preview_sheet": str(style_preview_sheet_path),
        },
    )


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage8_cover(*args, **kwargs)

def _assert_is_valid_png(path: Path) -> None:
    with Image.open(path) as img:
        assert img.format == "PNG"
        assert img.size == (1280, 720)


def test_stage8_writes_cover_overlay_manifest_and_preview_assets(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "stage8_contract"

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: False)

    result = stage8_cover.run_stage8_cover(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        forum_post_info={"cover_title_up": "涓绘爣棰?},
    )

    stage_dir = out_dir / task_id / "_stages"
    overlay_png = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_overlay.png"
    cover_image = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_image.png"
    cover_preview = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_preview.png"
    subtitle_preview = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_subtitle_preview.png"
    style_sheet = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_style_preview_sheet.png"
    overlay_manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_overlay_assets_manifest.json"

    assert result.success
    assert overlay_png.exists()
    assert cover_image.exists()
    assert cover_preview.exists()
    assert subtitle_preview.exists()
    assert style_sheet.exists()
    assert overlay_manifest.exists()
    _assert_is_valid_png(overlay_png)
    _assert_is_valid_png(cover_image)
    _assert_is_valid_png(cover_preview)
    _assert_is_valid_png(subtitle_preview)
    _assert_is_valid_png(style_sheet)

    payload = json.loads(overlay_manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload["schema_version"] == "1.0"
    assert payload["task_id"] == task_id
    assert payload["coordinate_space"] == "pixel_on_reference_canvas"
    assert payload["reference_video_role"] == "master_video"
    assert payload["canvas_width"] == 1280
    assert payload["canvas_height"] == 720

    assert payload["overlays"][0]["asset_id"] == "cover_overlay"

    assert payload["overlays"][0]["start"] == 0.0

    assert payload["overlays"][0]["z_index"] == 10
    assert payload["overlays"][0]["source"] == "generated"
